# cluster(C).id はそのつど変化する screで確認
#Command "select rowid,score(C),cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' clustered limit 0.98 order by rowid";
Command "select rowid,score(C) from T where C contains 'ロハス' clustered limit 0.98 order by rowid";

# ID, score, cluster.id を上でしているのでlimitの確認 
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 5";

Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 1";
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 2";
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 3";
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 4";

Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 1 offset 1";
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 2 offset 1";
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 3 offset 2";
Command "select cluster(C).id from T where C contains 'ロハス' limit 2 offset 3";
